54b1(phal chen): chos ston pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba la rjes su yi rang ba dang / dad cing mos pa dang / chung ngun ming brjod pa rgyas yang 'di ltar bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yom+b+ha/
54b2(phal chen): su smin pa'i phyir sems can rnams la don du 'gyur ba yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di lta ste/ dper na rje'i ming mthong na bde ba zhes bya ba de mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams kyi
54b3(phal chen): lus la zhen pa'am/ lhor zos pa'i dug rab tu zhi bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin du chos de lta bu dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yang mthong ma thag tu sems
54b4(phal chen): can rnams kyi nyon mongs pa'i dug thams cad byang bar 'gyur te/ chos dkar po'i stobs kyi shugs kyang skye bar 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems
54b5(phal chen): dpa' chen po chos nyid de lta bu dang ldan zhing chos de dag la gnas te/ shes rab kyi 'od chen pos ma rig pa'i mun pa bsal nas/ bdud kyi dkrugs ma'i 'khor thams cad byams
54b6(phal chen): pa dang snying rje chen po'i stabs kyis pham par byas te/ ye shes dang bsod nams kyi stobs kyi shugs kyis phas kyi rgol ba thams cad zil gyis mnan nas/ rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge
54b7(phal chen): 'dzin la 'jug pas/ sems kyi dri ma thams cad dang nyon mongs pa'i phyogs thams cad bsal nas/ skyo ba med pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba phun sum tshogs pa
55a1(phal chen): thams cad rab tu bsgrubs te/ sngun nad sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su drag par spyad pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis mi khos pa dang ngan so dang na 'grol
55a2(phal chen): lam thams cad rnam par bzlog nas/ mngon par zhen pa med pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor yongs su sbyangs te/ rim gyis thabs dang shes rab kyi stobs
55a3(phal chen): dang shugs kyis byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang pha rol tu phyin pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / mngon par shes dang / rig pa dang / mi 'jigs pa yongs su dag pa mngon par
55a4(phal chen): bsgrubs nas chos dkar po thams cad kyi stobs dang shugs kyis/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mtshan dang / dpe byad bzang po dang / sku dang / gsung dang / thugs
55a5(phal chen): kyi rgyun yongs su dag pa mngon par bsgrub pa rab tu rgyas par byas te/ ye shes kyis shes par bya ba'i dbang dang / byin gyis brlabs kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs dang // sangs rgyas
55a6(phal chen): kyi chos ma 'dres pa thams cad mnyam pa nyid khong du chud par byas nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyang myur du 'thob cing thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi
55a7(phal chen): yul yang sngon lam gyi khyad par ji lnga ba bzhin du 'brib par 'gyur ro// sngon gyi byin gyi rlabs dang ye shes kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis mngon par sangs rgyas nas/ sems can rnams kyi
55b1(phal chen): bsam pa sgri pa bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing bstan te 'dul bdi smra ba bzhin du sems can rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo chen po bskor cing / mtha' yas du'i mas sasmran
55b2(phal chen): par 'dul lo// kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i chos de lta bu dang ldan pa dag ni/ tshul de lta bus sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid kyi bar du thob par
55b3(phal chen): 'gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thob nas kyang / 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas pa dag tu dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin cing chos smra ba chen po'ang byed de// de ltar
55b4(phal chen): chos smra ba byed pa'i tshe// de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs pa de dag chos kyi mdzod chen po gzung zhing bsrung ba'i phyir
55b5(phal chen): so so yang dag par rig pas chos kyi tshul rab tu dbye ba'i rjes su song ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshig gis/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor mtha' yas par bdag gri lus kyi rkyen byin
55b6(phal chen): gyis brlabs te bstan pa mngon par bsgrub pa rnam po'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa dang / so so yang dag par rig pa'i mkhas pa mtha' yas pa dang / ye shes mi zad pa
55b7(phal chen): 'jug pa dang / dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor shin tu rnam par phye ba'i byin gyi rlabs dang / dbyangs gcig bsgrags pas/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad mgu bar byed pa'i
56a1(phal chen): dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa bsam pa dang / bag la nyal bdang / shes pa'i sa ji lta pa bzhin du rjes su 'drang ba dang / lus kyi rkyen gyis
56a2(phal chen): brlabs 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi nang du phyin kyang zil gyis mi non pa dang / lus kyi rgyan sgo thams cad du rnam par bstan pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi
56a3(phal chen): sems dang bsam pa khong du chud pas rab tu rtogs pa dang / tshig grol ba'i byin gyi rlabs kyis bstan pa dang / chos 'chad pa'i byin gyi rlabs la mkhas pas chos kyi gtam chen
56a4(phal chen): po byed de/ stobs dang shugs kyi dbang thub pa med pa dang / 'jigs pa med pa'i dbang zhum pa med pa dang / chos kyi dbang zil gyis mi non pa dang / ye shes kyi dbang gzhan gyis
56a5(phal chen): mi thub pa dang / shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i dbang chos kyi mtshan nyid 'khrugs pa med pa dang / so so yang dag par rig pa'i dbang mtshams sbyar ba rgyun chad pa med par bsam
56a6(phal chen): pa shin tu rtogs pa dang / gzungs kyi dbang chos thams cad rnam par gdon mi za ba la 'jug pa dang / smon lam gyi dbang dpe sna tshogs kyis bstan pa'i tshul nye bar bsgrub pa shin
56a7(phal chen): bstan pa dang / snying rje chen po'i dbang phyir mi ldog cing rgyun mchad pa dang / byams pa chen po'i dbang sngon shin tu bskyed pas bsam pa thams cad tshim par byed cing 'od zer gyi dri ba chen po gtong
56b1(phal chen): bas chos kyi gtam chen po byed do// de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge'i gudan la bzhugs shing chos kyi gtam gsung ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' ye shes dang smod lam gyi khyung
56b2(phal chen): par dang ldan pa ma gtogs par sems can gyi ris na byang chub sems dpa' de la byir brgal ba'am/ spyi gtsug blta ba'am/ zil gyis mnan pa'am/ dri ba'i tshogs yongs su dri bas
56b3(phal chen): thub par bya bar nus pa'i sems can gang yang med de/ de ni gnas med do// kyo rgyal ba'i sras gal te byang chub sems dpa' dbang de lta bu thob pa la / 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du mad
56b4(phal chen): btsam du yangs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor cig yod la/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de yang sems can stong gsum gyi bdag po'i gzi brjid thob pa sha stag gis gang bu zhig yin na yang / de dag
56b5(phal chen): thams cad byang chub sems dpa' 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du 'ongs ma thag tu lus bstan pa'i dbang gis zil gyis mnan te byams pa chen po'i dbang gis lus kyi gzhi tshim par byas nas
56b6(phal chen): ye shes chen po'i dbang gis sems dang bsamu pra rnam par shes par byas te/ mi 'jigs pa'i bsdam pa chen pos chos ston pa byed cing / spobs pa chen po'i dbang gis sems can
56b7(phal chen): tshim par byed do// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' de ni ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa dang ldan/ chos rnam par 'byed pa shin tu rnam
57a1(phal chen): par bye ba la mkhas pa dang ldan/ dran pa'i stobs dang shugs mnyams shing rgyame dang ldan/ nos thams cad kyi tshul rnam par gdod pa byung baju shing zlas ngas/
57a2(phal chen): rtogs par mkhas pa dang ldan// byang chub sems dpa'i thabs mkhas pa mtha' dang dbus med pa dang ldan/ chos kyi mtshan nyid bsgribs pa med pa'i chos ston pa la mkhris pad
57a3(phal chen): ldan mos pa la mkhas pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis blangs pa dang ldan/ dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor du yang dag par gzhol ba'i ye shes
57a4(phal chen): kyi byin gyis brlabs la mkhas pa dang ldan/ sems can thams cad kyi gtso bo 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba rnams dang / rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pa'i bsam pa bzang
57a5(phal chen): po rnam par dag pa la mkhas pa dang ldan pas chos smra ba chen po byed cing / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi chos kyi mdzod kyang rnam par 'byed do// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang
57a6(phal chen): da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi ye shes kyi byin gyis brlabs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i yid kyi smon lam dang / ye shes 'byam klas pas dam pa'i chos kyang yongs su
57a7(phal chen): 'dzin to// de nas byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyi blo gros kyis/ yang byang chub sems dpa' rim gyis yang dag par 'byung ba'i chos kyi sgo'i le'u yang dag par bstan
57b1(phal chen): pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// bsod nams tshogs bsags byang chub sems la gnas pa'i rnams/
57b2(phal chen): rtag tu bag yod blo brtan mthu tshon bdog pa dag/ dran dang ldan zhing byang chub sems rab mi gtong bas// phyogs rnams bcu por bde gshegs rnams ni mnyes par byed// brtson 'grus
57b3(phal chen): brnams pa dran ldan mos pa brtan pa can// 'jig rten kun la rtag tu mi gnas mi ldog pa// zab pa'i chos zhugs mya ngan med pa'i tshul mkhas rnams// phyogs rnams bcu bor ba
57b4(phal chen): gshegs rnams ni mnyes par byed// brtson 'grus brtan pas bde gshegs mnyes par byas nas kyang // dus gsum bsod nams tshogs dang ye shes ldan pa'i rnams/
57b5(phal chen): sa rnams gnon byed spyod mchog nyams pa med par byed// thub pa'i smon lam rdzogs byed ston pa'ang de bzhin byed// ye shes gcig la zhugs pa de dag thob bye ba// thob nas 'gro ba
57b6(phal chen): kun la sbyin pa rab tu gtong // bsam pa dag dang khams dang sbyor ba shes byas nas// dbang po ji bzhin mkhas pa de ltar chos kyang ston// pha rol phyin la brtson pa mthu chen ldan pa'i
57b7(phal chen): rnams// 'gro ba rnams la chos ston bdag gi don mi gtong // pha rol phyin rdzogs grol ba'i mthu chen ldan pa'i rnams// khyu mchog mthu yis 'khor ba'i mtsho las sems can
58a1(phal chen): sgrol/ de ltar nyin mtshan skyo ba med par brtson byed cing // drang srong rgyal ba chos rigs mi gcod zhugs pa yis// dkar po'i spyod pa gang yang rungs
58a2(phal chen): spyad pa'i rnams// thams cad don yod rgyal ba rnams kyi sar 'gro'o// de dag ci spyod thams cad 'gro ba rnams la yang // rnam smin don yod nyon mongs dri ma sbyong bar 'gyur// 'di
58a3(phal chen): 'dra'i chos ldan de dag mun pa bsal byas shing // bdud 'khrugs 'khor lo pham byas byang chub thob par byed// de ltar brtson zhing ye shes thob pa'i bde gshegs sras// bde gshegs
58a4(phal chen): rnams kyi chos rab mdzod kyang rab tu ston// de dag chos smra'i bya ba kun kyang shin tu byed// bdud rtsi mchog zhim sprin gyi char yang mngon par 'bebs// de dag snying rje byams pas 'gro ba kun
58a5(phal chen): bkang zhing // bstan pa de rnams 'khor gyi bsam pa shes byas nas// gang gi bsam pa blo gros sems rgyud ci 'dra ba// de bzhin rgyal bu'i chos ni stong phrag du ma ston// glang
58a6(phal chen): skabs sdug tshul bzang 'gros su 'gro ba'i rnams// seng ge'i rtsal ltar rtag tu sus kyang mi thub cing // ye shes rgya mtsho sa bur ri rab bzhin gnas pa// sprin lngar 'gro ba kun gyi
58a7(phal chen): nyin ma mo 'i byed/ khyeng dub sems dpa' chos kyi khri gros kyis de sang ces skyes pa dang / de la srid pas rjes su gyes pa mdzad // shin pa rgyas pachen pa'i mdas sa rgyas
58b1(phal chen): bal po che zhes bya ba las / chos snang ba'i le'u zhes bya ba ste nyi shu gsum pa'o// / de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi kham smra 'a sa
58b2(phal chen): cad dang / lho phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang / gzhung de bzhin du snang gi phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi bar thams cad na/ gling bzhi pa 'di la sogs pa gling bcu
58b3(phal chen): pa re re na de bzhin gshegs pa mang po bzhugs par snang ngo // byang chub sems dpa' de dag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs kyis chos ston to// bdag cag kyang de bzhin
58b4(phal chen): gshegs pa'i zhabs kyi drung na 'khod par shes so// bcom ldan 'das kyis rdzu 'phrul mngon par 'du mdzad pa ma bshig ma gtang bar byang chub kyi shing drung yang mu spangs par ri rab kyi rtsa
58b5(phal chen): mo nas mtshe ma'i gnas kyi lce'i bu rab mtshe ma'i khang pa nor bu sna tshogs gang na ba dor gshegs par snang ngo // ji ltar gling bzhi pa 'di ni bcom ldan 'das rab 'tshe ba'i gnas su gshi
58b6(phal chen): bar sdang bu de bzhin du/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na 'dra rab mtshe ma'i gnas su gshegs par snang ste/ byin gyi rlabs snga ma rnams kyang de bzhin ma 'khrugs par snang ngo /
58b7(phal chen): de nas lha'i rgyal po rib mtshems bcom ldan 'das rgyang ring po nas khang pa nor bu sna tshogs logs su mngon par gshegs pa mthong nas/ rings pa'i gzugs su khang pa nir dus
59a1(phal chen): tshogs kyi nang du de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdan rdzu 'phrul gyis bsgrubs pa'i seng ge'i khri pad+mo'i snying po can// lha rdzas kyi rin po che las byas bu brog
59a2(phal chen): brgya stong phrag bcus brgyan pa gser gyi dra ba brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas mngon par bros pa/ me tog gi bla re brgya stong phrag bcus kun tu khyab par byas pa/ 'phreng ba'i bla ra
59a3(phal chen): brgya stong phrag bcu kun tu brgyus pa/ spos kyi bla ro brgya stong phrag bcu sa spos thams cad kun tu 'thul bar bdugs pa/ rin po nA'i bla re brgya stong phrag bcus kun tu bres pa/
59a4(phal chen): me tog gi gdugs brgya stong phrag bcu kun nas bzung ba/ 'phreng ba'i gdugs brgya stong phrag bcu kun nas bzung ba dang / rin po che'i gdugs brgya stong phrag bcu kun nas bzung ba/
59a5(phal chen): 'od zer brgya stong phrag bcus snang bar byas pa/ rab mtshe ma'i lha'i rgyal po brgya stong phrag bcus rab tu btud pa/ tshangs pa brgya stong phrag bcus mngon par phyag byas pa/ byang chub
59a6(phal chen): sems dpa' brgya stong phrag bcus mngon par bstod pa/ rol mo brdung ba brgya stong phrag bcu'i sgra phyung ba/ chos kyi klu'i dbyangs brgya stong phrag bcu'i gru'i dbyangs dang ldan pa/ mi tog
59a7(phal chen): gi sprin gi char brgya snying brag bcu rab tu phab pa/ 'phreng ba'i sprin gyi cher ba rgya snying phrag bcu rab tu bab pa/ rgyun gyi snod brgya stong phrag bcu rab tu papo pa// gos kyi skyon gyi char ba
59b1(phal chen): ga rna pa gas / na pa sprin ga sa shA pa/ gle smrasu
59b2(phal chen): nas byung ba/ sangs rgyas brgya steng phrag bcus byin gyis 'arlabs pa/ bsod nams brgya stong phrag bcus bsags shing bsgrubs pa/ lhag pa'i bsapa pa brgya stong phrag bdus zhing
59b3(phal chen): du sbyangs pa/ spor lam brgya sdong brag bcus rnam par dag par byas pa/ spyod pa brgya stong phrag bcus kun nas bsrung ba/ chos brgya stong phrag bcus rab tu bstan pa/ rnam par 'phrul
59b4(phal chen): ba brgya stong phyag bcu dang ldan pa/ yon tan brgya stong phrag bcus shin tu 'phags pa/ brjod pa brgya stong phrag bcus shin tu brjod pa ba shams so// ji ltar gleng bzhi pa 'di rab
59b5(phal chen): ma'i gnas kyi lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe ma'i khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdan bting ba de bzhin du/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi grong bzhi pa dag gi rab mtshe ma'i
59b6(phal chen): gnas su yang / khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe ma rnams kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdan rgyun 'di 'dra ba dang / bshams pa'i tshul 'di 'dra ba dag kyang bting
59b7(phal chen): bar gyur to// de nas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshems bcom ldan 'das kyi gdan bting nas/ zhes dang rim gror bcom ldan 'das gang na ba de legs su thal mo sbyar te phyag 'tshal nas/
60a1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das gshegs su gsol/ bde bar gshegs pa gshegs su gsol/ de bzhin gshegs
60a2(phal chen): pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i srungs rgyas bde bur gshegs sram/ de nas bcom ldan 'das lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe mus spyan drangs pa bzhin du khyang pa nor bu sna tshogs su
60a3(phal chen): gshegs so// ji ltar gling bzhi pa 'dir rab mtshe ma'i gnas su lha'i rgyal po rab mtshe ma'i khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su gshegs pa de bzhin du/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams
60a4(phal chen): cad du'ang rab mtshe ma'i gnas kyi khang pa nor bu sna tshogs su gshegs par snang ngo // de nas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshems lha'i dbang po'i gnas thams cad du sgra bsgrags te
60a5(phal chen): lha'i rgyal po rab mtshems/ bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba btang // de nas lha'i rgyal po rab mtshems sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
60a6(phal chen): pa'i sangs rgyas rnams la dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa de rjes su dran nas/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// bkra shis
60a7(phal chen): dam pa gang zhig gis// sangs rgyas grags pa'i dang par mtshan btags mtshan gsol ba// nor bu'i gtsug tu gshegs pa ltar// des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur/
60b1(phal chen): cig/ bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis// 'jig rten sgron ma blo zhes mtshan btags pa// sbyangs pa'i lam du gshegs pa ltar// des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur
60b2(phal chen): cig/ bkra shris dam pa gang zhig gis// bsgribs med gzigs pa 'dzum pa'i spyan du mtshan btags pa// rgyan gcig ldan par gshegs pa ltar// des ni 'dir yang /
60b3(phal chen): shis mchog gyur cig/ dkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis// 'jig rten sgron ma mar me mdzad ces mtshan btags pa// rnam par rgyal bar gshegs pa ltar// des ni 'dir
60b4(phal chen): yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig/ bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis// bde gshegs yang dag don gzigs pa zhes mtshan btags pa// dri med rtse mor gshegs pa ltar//
60b5(phal chen): des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig/ bkra shis dam pa grang zhig gis// de bzhin gshegs pa rang byung mchog ces mtshan btags pa// rin chen spros su gshegs
60b6(phal chen): pa ltar// des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig/ bkra shis dam pa grang zhig gis// 'jig rten sgron ma dbyig gi lha zhes mtshan btags pa// dri med sna tshogs/
60b7(phal chen): gshegs pa ltar// des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig/ bkra shis das pa gang zhig gis// 'gro ba med pa spa ba'i stag ces mtshan btags pa// thams cad
61a1(phal chen): tshul du gshegs pa ltar// des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig/ bkra shis dam pa gang zhig gis// yon tan kun mnga' dpal gyis rgyas par
61a2(phal chen): mtshan btags pa// dga' ba'i rgyan du gshegs pa ltar// des ni 'drir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig/ bkra shis dram pa gang zhig gis// 'jig rten phan brtson dka' thub/
61a3(phal chen): drug por mtshan btags pa// kun nas mdog tu gshegs pa ltar/ des ni 'dir yang bkra shis mchog gyur cig/ ji ltar lha'i rgyal po rab mtshem sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs
61a4(phal chen): kyis sngon gyi rgyal ba'i gshegs pa brjod de mngon par bstod pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rgyal po rab mtshe ma rnams kyang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis
61a5(phal chen): sngon gyi yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gshegs pa brjod cing / glu'i dbyangs kyis tshigs su bcad de mngon par bstod do// de nas bcom ldan 'das khang po nor bu sna tshogs
61a6(phal chen): su gshegs nas gdan bting ba la skyil mo krung bcas te bzhugs so// ji ltar bcom ldan 'das bzhugs pa de bzhin du/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du yang gting ba de dag la
61a7(phal chen): bzhugs par snang ngo // bcom ldan 'das bzhugs ma thag tu khang pa nor bu sna tshogs de 'di lta ste/ dper na rab mchi ma'i lha'i ris thams cad tsam du che bar gyur par snang ste
61b1(phal chen): 'di na ji lta ba bzhin 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na'ang de bzhin no// shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ rab mtshe ma'i gnas na rnam par 'phrul
61b2(phal chen): ba'i le'u zhes bya ba ste nyi shu bzhi pa'o// de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcu nas byang chub sems dpa' mang po lhags par gyur te/ byang chub sems
61b3(phal chen): dpa' re re zhing yang 'khor sangs rgyas kyi zhing brgya phrag stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu 'ongs te/ byang chub sems dpa' re re zhing yang byang chub sems dpa' sangs kyi zhing gi
61b4(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang lhan cig tu byin to// byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad kyang ming 'di zhes bya ba dag ste/ 'di ltar yon tan dang ldan pa dang / blo gros dang ldan pa dang /

76a4(phal chen): med par yang mtshams med cing ngal mi shes/ skyo mi shes/ rgyun mi 'chad/ gtong ba med/ sdod pa med/ gcugs su med/ dbugs 'byin pa med/ phyir sri ba med par btags
76a5(phal chen): kyang kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ de lta bu'i 'dzegs pa chen po mi bzad pa/ ma rus pa// skyi g.ya' ba/ sdug bsngal ba/ nyams su 'bab pa/ che ba/ rtsub pas phog
76a6(phal chen): sde srog la bab par 'chim khad kyang / de la byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam du sems te/ sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa 'di tsam dag gis phog pa la/ gal te bdag gis sems 'ju
76a7(phal chen): pa nig byas su zin na/ de ni mdus pa dang / mi bdond pa dang / mi mkhas pa dang / mning dang / ma bsgoms pa dang / ma bsdams pa dang / mkhrugs pa dang / byas kyi/
76b1(phal chen): med pa dang / mnyam par ma bzhag pa dang / bdag gi lus la brten pas gzhan gyi sa mas mgu ba dpya bar mi nus kyis shes te/ de lus dang sems kyi rang ba'idi shes nas/ thog pa
76b2(phal chen): dang tha ma med par skye ba dang / 'khor ba'i sdug bsngal rjes su dran nas/ chos 'di dag gi tshul gyis de bzhin no zhes nas/ phyir ni sems dang bar byed/ rab tu dang bar byed/ dga' bar
76b3(phal chen): byed/ rab tu dga' bar byed/ tshim par byed/ gzengs mtho bar byed/ spro bar byed/ rab tu spro bar byed/ 'dul bar byed/ yongs su 'dems par byed/ de ltar bdag gis kyang
76b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos la bzhag ste/ sems can thams cad la yang don 'di nyid bstan par bya'o snyam mo// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar lus 'di ni badrag dang bdag gis stong pa ste/
76b5(phal chen): bzhin gyis stong pa'o// stong pa nyid la ni bde ba 'am/ sdug bsngal ba'am/ gnyis su brjod pa gang yang med do// gang stong pa de la ci yang med de/ chos thams cad ni
76b6(phal chen): yang ma yin pa yin gyi// de bdag gis kyang yang dag par shes par byas te/ sems can thams cad la dngos por 'dzin pa spang ba'i phyir chos bstan par bya dgos kyi/ de ltar bdag gis
76b7(phal chen): 'di dag la byams pa'i sems dang / phan pa'i sems dang / bde ba'i sems dang / snying rje ba'i semra dang / snying brtse ba'i sems dang / phan par dga' ba'i sems dang / yongs su mi gtong ba'i
77a1(phal chen): sems dang / 'tshang rgya ba'i sems dang / byang chub pa'i sems dang / mi 'phrogs pa'i sems dang / sangs rgyas kyi tshul gyis rjes su bsnyegs pa'i

77a3(phal chen): med pa zhes bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bzhi po mi zad pa zhes bya ba de gang zhe na/
77a4(phal chen): 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po brtson 'grus dang ldan pa yin te/ brtson 'grus mchog dang ldan pa yin/ brtson 'grus rab dang ldan pa yin/ brtson 'grus dam pa dang ldan
77a5(phal chen): pa yin/ brtson 'grus phul dang ldan pa yin/ brtson 'grus 'phags pa dang ldan pa yin/ brtson 'grus gya nom pa dang ldan pa yin/ brtson 'grus bla na med pa dang ldan pa yin/ brtson
77a6(phal chen): 'grus mi nyam pa dang ldan pa yin te/ de la 'dod chags kyi rang bzhin med/ zhe sdang gi rang bzhin med/ gti mug gi rang bzhin med/ dargyal gyi rang bzhin med/ 'chab pa'i rang ba zhin med/
77a7(phal chen): brag gag ba'i med/ 'jus pa'i rang bzhin med/ spu ma'i rang bani ming / sku'i rang bzhin meng/ khrel med pa'i rang banini med do// doni sems can gang sa yang mtho btsam pa'i
77b1(phal chen): phyir brtsor 'grus ma rtsoms/ gzhan dun can mongs pa rnams cad yongs su spang ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rlom ma// bag sa zhal ba thams cad yang dag par gas pa'i nga rlos 'grus
77b2(phal chen): rtsom mo// bag chags thams cad yongs su bsal ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo// sems can gyi khams yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus tsamam// shi 'thod sbyir
77b3(phal chen): thams cad yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo// nyon mongs pa thams cad yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo// sems can gyi bsam pa thams cad yongs
77b4(phal chen): su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo// sems can thams cad kyi spyod yul yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo// sems can thams cad kyi dbang po dang brtson
77b5(phal chen): 'grus rnam pa tha dad pa mchog dang tha mo'i rgyus yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo// sems can thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo//
77b6(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings thams cad la 'jug pa yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin dang ngo bo nyid yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson
77b7(phal chen): 'grus rtsom mo// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo// dus gsum la mkhas pa mnyam pa nyid yongs su shes par bya
78a1(phal chen): ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad shes pa'i snang ba mnyam pa nyid yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom// sas

78a3(phal chen): shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo// sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' dang dbus med pa thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya ba yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom mo// sangs

78a5(phal chen): rab tu bstan pa'i rgyus yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus rtsom ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras drug/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni de lta bu'i brtson 'grus dang ldan pa
78a6(phal chen): yin no// de gal te 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med pa'i sems can rnams kyi don du sems can re re'i phyir yang bskal pa grangs med par mnar med pa'i sems can dmyal ba chen por sdug
78a7(phal chen): bsngal du 'dug par yang spro zhing mos te/ sems can de dag kyang de tsam gyi bar gyis yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bar gyur la/ de'i dus su sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das grangs med pa zhig
78b1(phal chen): byungaste/ sangs rgyas banam ldan 'das de dag sus mthong ba de dgra thams cad kyang 'dre ba'i yo byud kun da nga ldan par byu // rlung chub sems dpa 'dren med pa sa dag pa tsunas
78b2(phal chen): pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang mi rgya dang / byang chub sems dpa' di ni 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med par gtogs pa'i sems can rnams kyi spyi / sems can
78b3(phal chen): don du yang bskal pa grangs med pa sems can dmyal ba chen po ni de snyed kyi sems can yongs su mya ngan las 'das kyi bar du 'dug par smra smra/ de la la la zhig gis 'di skad du
78b4(phal chen): mtsho chen po grangs med pa skra'i rtse mos gzhal te/ 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med pa rdul du brlags te bgrang ba snyed kyi sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba dang / sems skad cig tu yang mi 'bral
78b5(phal chen): ba'i sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa de lta bu dang mi 'bral bar 'gyur ro zhes zer na yang / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang chub sems dpa' ni de la de'i phyir sems bskyed pa 'ga' tsam yang 'gyod
78b6(phal chen): pa dang ldan pa mi 'byung gi/ de ni 'di snyam ste/ de ltar bdag gi mthus sems can 'di dag sdug bsngal gyi rnam pa de lta bu las yongs su 'grol bar 'gyur ba ni/ bdag gis 'thob pa
78b7(phal chen): legs par 'thob bo// gal te thabs 'di 'dra bas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can thams cad yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bar 'gyur na yang / byang chub sems dpas
79a1(phal chen): spong ba de la sngo ba dbya ba yin no zhes te/ de bas kyang ches dga' ba slob ste'o// ce rgyal ba'i sras da/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
79a2(phal chen): rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa ba'i paste/ mi zang pa zhes bya bya'o// me rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub sems
79a3(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa lnga pa rmongs pa med pazhes bya ba gang rten/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' dran pa dang ldan pa yin te/ dran pa'i ngas pa 'khrug pa med do/ rnam par
79a4(phal chen): 'khrug pa med pa/ brtan pa/ sra ba/ mi shigs pa/ zil gyis mi non pa/ yongs su dag pa/ che ba/ tshad med pa/ rmongs pa med pa dang ldan pa yin te/ dran pa des
79a5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi spyod pa rnams kyang yongs su 'dzin pa yin/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i tshig kyang yongs su 'dzin pa yin/ gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i tshig kyang yongs su 'dzin pa
79a6(phal chen): yin/ gzugs kyi rang bzhin la btags pa'i tshig kyang yongs su 'dzin pa yin/ tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang / 'du byed dang / rnam par shes pa la btags pa'i tshig kyang
79a7(phal chen): yongs su 'dzin pa yin/ rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin yongs su shes par bya ba'i phyir tshig kyang yongs su 'dzin pa yin te/ de 'jig rten 'di nas kyang rmongs pa med par shi 'phol/

79b6(phal chen): sems dpa'i rgyan gyi chos sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs snang ba can nam/ bla na med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos lhug pa'i bsam pa dge ba dang mos pas rnam par dag pa 'am/ 'jig rten thams

83a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos kyang 'jig rten gyi chos su rab tu 'jug go// 'jig rten gyi chos kyang sangs rgyas kyi chos su rab du 'jug go// sas rgyas kyi chos dang 'dzin

83a4(phal chen): phyir snying rje chen po yang phyir zhing rab tu 'dzin par byed do// sems can gyi khams bdag gis smin par ma byas pa ni su zhig smin par byed/ sems can gyi khams bdag gis dul bar ma

83b1(phal chen): par gyur pa/ tshor ba nyams su bab pa/ mi bzad pas nad par gyur pa/ sred pas bskor ba'i banon ra zhugs pa/ sems can dmyal ba dang rgyal song gi skye gdus pa
83b2(phal chen): gshin rje'i 'jig rten las ma g.yos pa/ sdug bsngal gyi phung pos ma skyo ba/ sdom pa gsum gyis gcugs su ma rung ba/ mun nug gi nang du rab tu zhugs pa/ ma rig pa'i mngal du

83b5(phal chen): 'di ltar skye ste/ de ltar bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu zhugs te/ ye shes kyi snang ba bla na med pa la zhugs nas sems can 'di dag yongs su ma smin cing /

90b1(phal chen): bzang po'i chos la spyod pa'i tshe/ spyod do zhes bya bar mi dmigs so// spyad do zhes bya bar mi dmigs so// spyad par bya'o zhes bya bar mi dmigs so// khams kyi yul dang
90b2(phal chen): skye mched kyi yul da / rlung gi snang ba dang / phyi rol gyi snang ba dang / byi rlung gi sdang ba dang / srod la yongs su bsgrub pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa rnams dang / chos thams cad
90b3(phal chen): yang mi dmigs so// de ci'i phyir ni ma/ 'di ltar chos kyi dbyings thams cad la ni gang nyan thos kyi theg pa la zhugs pa'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la zhugs pa 'am/ byang chub
90b4(phal chen): sems dpa'i theg pa la zhugs pa 'am// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu zhugs pa 'am/ so so'i skye bo'i khams la zhugs pa 'am/ kun nas nyon mongs pa'i khams
90b5(phal chen): la zhugs pa 'am/ rnam par byang ba'i khams la zhugs pa 'am/ 'khor ba'i khams la zhugs pa 'am/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i khams la zhugs pa'i chos gang yang med do//
90b6(phal chen): de yang ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di la chos gnyis shes bya ba yang med de/ mi gnyis pa yang med do// 'di lta ste/ dper du ram mkha' ni phyogs bcur ma rnyed/ mi rnyed/ rnyed par mi
90b7(phal chen): 'gyur na yang / nam mkhar bgrang ba'i tshul yod do// de bzhin du byang chub sems dpas kyang chos gang yang dmigs pa med do// chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya'o zhes grangs
91a1(phal chen): su bgrang ba'ang yod de/ de ni yang dag pa bded pa ste/ log pa ma yin no// de ni bya ba dang mi 'gal ba'i spyod pa yang ston to// smon lam yang mi
91a2(phal chen): gtong ngo // sems can gyi khams yongs su smin pa dang 'dul ba yang byed do// chos kyi 'khor lo yang skor ro// rgyu dang 'bras bu yang 'jig par mi byed do// chos nyid dang yang
91a3(phal chen): 'gal bar mi byed do// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang yang mnyam par 'gyur ba yin te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyang
91a4(phal chen): rgyun chad par mi byed/ chos kyi tshul dang yang 'gal bar mi byed/ chos kyi rgyud kyang rab tu shes so// chos kyi spobs pa yang 'jig par mi byed/ chos thos pas kyang rlom sems
91a5(phal chen): med de/ chos kyi 'byung gnas kyang rab tu thob/ chos brjod pa'ang rab tu byed/ mi 'jigs pa la yang rab tu gnas/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'ang mi gtong ngo // 'jig rten gyi
91a6(phal chen): tshul yang 'gog par mi byed/ 'jig rten mnyam pa nyid kyang rab tu ston te/ 'jig rten gyi spyod pa rnams la yang gnas pa med do// de ltar byang chub sems dpa' thub par dka' ba'i
91a7(phal chen): sems dang ldan pa byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa la spyod de/ sems can gyi khams kyang sems can dmyal ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten nas gyen du
91b1(phal chen): spyod de/ de dag bskyod nas kyang yongs su smin par byed do// 'dul bar byed do// rab tu gnog par byed do// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom
91b2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi lam gyi rgyud las kyang mi g.yo'o// 'jig rten gnas pa drin du mi gzo bas yongs su gang ba dang / dgras yongs su gang ba dang / kun nas nyon mongs pas yongs su
91b3(phal chen): gang ba dang / mi mthun pas yongs su gang ba dang / yid gzhag tu mi rung bas yongs su gang ba dang / byis pas yongs su grang ba dang / ma dad pas yongs su gang ba dang / gzhan gyi drang
91b4(phal chen): la rgyug pas yongs su gang ba dang / shes rab ngan pas shin tu byung ba dang / 'jig rten gnas pa sred pa'i bsam pa dang / ma rig pas kun nas nyon mongs par gyur pa na/ byang chub sems
91b5(phal chen): dpa'i ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod de/ de 'di snyam du sems so// 'di ltar bdag gis 'jig rten gnas pa drin du gzo bas yongs su gang ba dang / mdza' bos yongs su gang ba dang
91b6(phal chen): mkhas pas yongs su gang bar byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyad pa lnga ngo mtshar du'ang ci che ste/ de ji lta zhe na/ bdag ni sems can mdza' ba'am mi mdza' ba gang las kyang chung ngun skra'i rtse mo
91b7(phal chen): gcig tsam mam/ chung ngu na dge bar bya ba sbyin pa tsam yang mi 'dod mi tshol te/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal par byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod kyang / gzhan du na sems can de dag
92a1(phal chen): yongs su dgrol ba dang / sems can de dag yongs su dad par 'gyur ba dang / sems can de dag 'byung bar 'gyur ba ma gtogs par// de dag las sems skad cig tsam du
92a2(phal chen): bde bar 'gyur ba'ang mi tshol lo// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bdag ni sems la len pa med cing thams cad la 'dod pa med pas/ sems can gyi gtso bor 'gyur bar byed pa ste/ 'di ltar bdag gis ci
92a3(phal chen): nas kyang sems can de dag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi mthas gtugs te/ shin tu bde ba'i pha rol tu phyin par 'gyur bar nan tan bya'o snyam mo// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/
92a4(phal chen): 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa brgyad pa ste/ thub par dka' ba zhes bya'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang
92a5(phal chen): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dgu pa chos bzang po zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa'
92a6(phal chen): lha dang 'jig rten du bcas pa/ bdud du bcas pa/ tshangs par bcuso pa/ dge sbyong dang bram zer bcas pa'i skye dgu lha dang / dri za dang / mi dang / lha ma yin du bcas
92a7(phal chen): pa na/ chos kyi mu stegs bzang por gyur pa yin te/ de sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcad pa'i phyir dam pa'i chos yongs su 'dzin par byed pa yin/ gzungs kyi snang ba rnam par dag pa thob
92b1(phal chen): pas gtam bya ba dang / lung bstan pa la spobs pa yin/ chos dang ldan pa'i gzungs thob pas don la spobs pa yin/ chos ji lta ba bzhin gyi gzus chos yang dag par skul pa thob pas/
92b2(phal chen): chos la spobs pa yin// tshig dang smra ba thams cad kyi gzungs rab tu thob pas nges pa'i tshig la spobs pa yin/ tshig dang yi ge'i don kun tu mtha' yas shing zad mi shes pa la thogs
92b3(phal chen): pa med pa'i sgo'i gzungs thob pas spobs pa thogs pa med pa yin/ sangs rgyas dbang bskur ba'i gzungs kyi dbang bskur bas mngon par dga' bar byed pa'i spobs pa dang ldan pa yin/
92b4(phal chen): gnan gyi dring la mi 'jog pa'i gzungs kyi sgro thob pas snang ba thob pa'i spobs pa dang ldan pa yin/ spobs pa thun mo nga ba'i tshul la zhugs pas thun mong gi spobs pa dang ldan pa yin/
92b5(phal chen): don mang po dang / tshig mang po dang / yi ge mang po de dang de drag la nges pa'i tshig gis gzungs kyi sgor chud pas nges pa'i spobs pa dang ldan pa yin/ rgyud mtha' yas pa'i gzungs
92b6(phal chen): thob pas mtha' yas pa'i spobs pa dang ldan pa yin te/ des ni stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi don du bdag gi lus gser gyi mdog tu mngon par sprul nas/ chos
92b7(phal chen): 'byam klas pa thams cad dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi sgo thams cad du chud pas sems can de dang ngag 'dul ba'i dbang du bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du brjod pa dang / dbang po 'byam klas pa
93a1(phal chen): mtha' yas pa rnams la// lce yangs pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa dang / dus dang 'byor pa'i chos bstan pa dang / snying
93a2(phal chen): rje chen po 'gal ba med pas shin tu bstan pa dang / tshig gcig gi sgra brjod pas 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du tshim par 'gyur zhing / mtha' yas par snang bar ston pas sangs rgyas kyi
93a3(phal chen): mdzad pa la spyod do// de ni 'gal te sems can re re zhing tshig rnam pa tha dad pa'i tshig gi cho ga las sna tshogs kyis mngon par 'du byas pa/ rnam par smin pa brjod kyis mi lang zhing 'byam klas
93a4(phal chen): pas nye bar gnas pa/ bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ grangs med pa/ rnam par phye ba/ rnam pa mtha' dad pa/ brjod du med pa dang ldan pa de lta bu'i sems
93a5(phal chen): can sha stag byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor du gyur la/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yang 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa tsam du yangs pa zhig yin te/ 'dul ba brjod du med pa zhig
93a6(phal chen): 'dus nas/ sems can re re la yang kha'i sgo bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa brjod du med pa yod par gyur te/ sems can gcig ji lta bar sems can de dag thams cad kyang
93a7(phal chen): de bzhin du de snyed kyi kha'i sgo dang ldan la/ sems can de dag thams cad kyis byang chub sems dpa' la skad du brjod pa/ bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa rnam par brtags
93b1(phal chen): pas dus gcig tu dbyangs gcig tu byas te yongs su dri ba byas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' ni de lta bu'i sems can gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa dang / de lta bu'i skad gcig nas
93b2(phal chen): gcig tu brgyud pa dang / de lta bu'i brjod pa sna tshogs kyis yongs su dris pa la'ang chos gzung ba la thogs pa med pa yin/ brjod pa shes par bya ba'i phyir rnam par rtog pa med pa yin te/
93b3(phal chen): dri bas the tshom yongs su dris pa la thogs pa med do// 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gcig tu ji lta ba de bzhin du/ 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor brjod du med pa de tsam thams cad du'ang de bzhin te/
93b4(phal chen): de la byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam du sems so// gal te skra'i rtse mo re re la sems bskyed pa re re zhing 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor brjod du med pa zhig byung la/ sems skad cig re re la rtog pa
93b5(phal chen): gnan dang gzhan gyis skud gzhan dang gzhan du brjod pas/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad gang bar byed cing 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnam pa de lta bu sha stag gis skra'i rtse mo thams cad la byung ste//
93b6(phal chen): de ltar byung bas phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par byung yang 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor de dag 'byung bas/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par zad par gyur te/ 'khor de rnams ni
93b7(phal chen): zang mi shes par byung la/ skye ba'i rgyun mi 'chang pa zhig yod du zin na yang / bstan par bya ba'i sa de la byang chub sems dpa' sems skad cig pa 'ga' tsam du yang num pa mi skye'o//
94a1(phal chen): snyom pa mi skye'o// snying skur ba dpa la snyom pa mi skye'o// the tshom dang yid gnyis mi skye'o// bag tsha ba dang 'jigs pa mi skye'o// rmongs pa dang 'khrul pa mi
94a2(phal chen): skye'o// byang chub sems dpa' chos bzang po la gnas pa de ni 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag gis sems can 'di dag dang / sems can gzhan rnams dang / sems can gyi khams
94a3(phal chen): thams cad kyang tshig gi las kyis yongs su mgu bar byas te/ chos bshad pa'i mthar thug par mi bya/ chos la rnam par thogs par mi bya'o zhes nas/ des brjod pa de dag thams cad
94a4(phal chen): kyang rab tu shes te/ sems can de dag la brtag mi dgos par 'byung ba'i tshig dang / tshig gis cho ga rnam pa tha dad pa brtag mi dgos par 'byung ba dang / tshig gis rnam par gdags pa brjod
94a5(phal chen): du med pa'i yang brjod du med par 'byung bas chos ston par byed do// de brjod pa de dag thams cad kyang 'dzin la/ sems kyi skad cig gcig gis kyang tshig thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du dbang
94a6(phal chen): bskur ba chags pa med pa'i snying po can/ chos thams cad kyi snang ba rab tu thob pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la gzhol ba gcig gis sems can thams cad kyang go bar byed do//
94a7(phal chen): de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa chos bzang po la gnas pa ni mngon par chags pa med pa'i tshul gyis bdag rnam par dag pa yang rab tu 'thob bo//
94b1(phal chen): sems can med par 'byung ba'i tshul gyis sems can thams cad kyi don yang yongs su rdzogs par byed do// de ni dus gcig tu stong gsum pa bcu nas/ stong gsum pa brjod kyis mi
94b2(phal chen): lang ba'i don du byin gyis brlabs shing / bdag gi lus gser gyi mdog tu mngon par sprul to/ dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad shes pa'i sgor chud pa chos thams cad du khyab pas/
94b3(phal chen): mtha' dang dbus med pa'i chos kyi sgor 'jug cing sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las bsgrub ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyu ba 'gags pas 'gro ba med pa'i lus rnams dang
94b4(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad du 'byung bas mtha' yas par 'gro ba'i lus rnams dang / mi skye ba dang mnyam pa'i chos la brtson pas ma skyes pa'i lus rnams dang / 'gog par brjod pa thams
94b5(phal chen): cad dmigs pa med pas 'gags pa med pa'i lus rnams dang / ji lta ba bzhin du dmigs pas bden pa med pa'i lus rnams dang / 'jig rten gyi bden pa bzhin du rnam par dmigs
94b6(phal chen): pas mi slu ba'i lus rnams dang / 'chi 'pho ba dang skye ba las 'das pas mi 'pho ba'i lus rnams dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi rang bzhin 'jig par mi byed pas mi 'jig pa'i lus rnams/
94b7(phal chen): dang / dus gsum gyi tshig gi lam la brtson pas skad cig gcig gi lus rnams dang / chos kyi mtshan nyid shin tu rtogs pa'i mthar thug pas mtshan nyid med pa'i lus rnams dang /
95a1(phal chen): lus rnam par phye ba 'byam klas pa bcu po de dag dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad bskyed pa la sems can thams cad kyi gnas yin no//
95a2(phal chen): dbugs chen po phyin par bya ba la sems can tham cad kyi dpung gnyen yin no// gnas chen po thob par bya ba la sems can thams cad kyi skyobs yin no// bla na med pa'i 'byung ba mthong
95a3(phal chen): bar bya ba la sems can thams cad kyi rten yin no// chos kyi tshul la 'jug par bya ba la sems can thams cad kyi 'dren pa yin no// las kyi rnam par smin pa rnam par dmigs par bya ba
95a4(phal chen): la sems can thams cad kyi me mar yin no// chos zab mo rab tu thob par bya ba la 'jig rten thams cad kyi snang ba yin no// chos thams cad ji lta ba bzhin du rmongs pa med par khong du
95a5(phal chen): chud par bya ba la khams gsum thams cad kyi sgron me yin no// snang ba'i sa rab tu 'thob par bya ba la 'jig rten thams cad kyi snang ba yin no// sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa
95a6(phal chen): yang dag par bstan par bya ba la 'gro ba thams cad rab tu dga' ba yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub sems
95a7(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa dgu pa chos bzang po zhes bya ba ste/ de la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad du 'jug par bya ba la
95b1(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad kyi mu stegs yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bcu pa bden pa dang /
95b2(phal chen): ldan pa zhes bya ba gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' bden pa'i tshig dam pa dang ldan pas bden pa'i tshig can yin te/ de ni gang smras pa de byed/ gang
95b3(phal chen): byed pa de smra'o// de 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bden pa'i gsung la yang slob bo// ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bden pa'i gsung
95b4(phal chen): la yang slob bo// da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bden pa'i gsung la'ang slob bo// 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rigs
95b5(phal chen): la yang 'jug go// ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rigs la yang 'jug go// da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rigs la'ang 'jug go/
95b6(phal chen): 'das pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'ang 'thob bo// ma byon pa de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'ang 'thob bo// da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin
95b7(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba'ang 'thob bo// de ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba thams cad dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba lhan gcig
96a1(phal chen): tu gyur pa ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rjes su bslabs pa'i ye shes dang ldan pas gnyis su med par smra ba yin no// de sems can rnams kyi gnas dang gnas
96a2(phal chen): ma yin pa'i shes pa la'ang rab tu 'jug go// de sems can rnams kyi 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i las rnam par smin pa shes pa la'ang rab tu 'jug go// dbang po
96a3(phal chen): dang brtson 'grus rnam pa tha dad pa rdzogs pa dang / ma rdzogs pa dang / rab dang tha ma shes pa la yang rab tu 'jug go// khams tha dad pa dang / khams du ma la yang rab tu 'jug go// mos
96a4(phal chen): pa tha dad pa dang / mos pa du ma la'ang rab tu 'jug go// thams cad du 'gro ba'i lam gyi ye shes la'ang rab tu 'jug go// bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / ting nge 'dzin dang /
96a5(phal chen): sgom par 'jug pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba rnam par dgod pa sems can rnams kyi dus dang dus ma yin par byung ba'ang rab tu shes so// 'jig rten gyi khams
96a6(phal chen): 'byam klas pa thams cad du sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa'i shes pa lo'ang rab tu 'jug go// lha'i mig chags pa med pa yang mngon par sgrub bo// zag pa zad pa shes pa'ang rab tu shes te/
96a7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa nye bar gzung ba'ang rgyun mi gcod do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni 'gro ba thams cad rnam par dag par bya ba dang gdul ba'i phyir zhugs pa
96b1(phal chen): yin te/ de phyir zhing sems 'di snyam du skye'o// 'di ltar 'jig rten gnas pa yongs su ma grol bar/ bdag rnam par grol ba'i tshul rab tu shes par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad
96b2(phal chen): yongs su ma bkrol zhing smon lam rjes su ma bsrungs par/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya ba 'di ni bdag la michis/ de bas na
96b3(phal chen): ci nas kyang sems can 'di dag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi mthas gtugs par 'gyur ba dang / gang 'di phung po'i lhag ma ma lus pa'i mya ngan las 'dras pa'i dbyings kyi
96b4(phal chen): mthar thug par gzhol bar 'gyur ba de ltar bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bdag cag ni sems can thams cad kyis gsol ba ma btab pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen te/ sems can thams
96b5(phal chen): cad kyis ma bskul bar yang dag par zhugs pa/ sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba la thog mar 'gro ba'o// bdag cag ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la 'jug pa'i phyir kha lo sgyur ba ste
96b6(phal chen): bdag cag ni 'gro ba kun gyis gos pa med pa'i phyir mchog tu gyur pa'o// bdag cag ni bla na med par kha lo sgyur ba'i sa la dam par gyur pa'o// bdag cag ni sems can med pa'i mtha' la
96b7(phal chen): rab ba med pa'o// bdag cag ni sngon gyi smon lam gyis thob pa dang ldan pa'o// bdag cag ni byang chuba'i sems dpa'i yon tan gyi rgyan thams cad kyis shin tu sprul pa'o// bdag cag
97a1(phal chen): ni sangs rgyas 'das pa dang / ma byo pa dang / dA ltar byung ba thams cad kyis yongs su bzung ba'i nas d+he/ de sngon gyi smod lam yang rig par mi byed do//
97a2(phal chen): bla na med pa'i ye shes kyi rgyan la yang rab tu 'jug go// sems can thams cad kyi don yang yongs su rdzogs par byed do// sngon gyi smon lam ji ltar btab pa yang thog ma dang / bar dang
97a3(phal chen): tha ma'i tshul gyis yongs su rdzogs par byas nas 'gro ba thams cad rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir/ chos thams cad shes pa'i mngon par shes pa'ang rab tu thob par byed do// sems bskyed pa re re zhing
97a4(phal chen): yang phyogs bcur rgyas par 'gro sta/ sems bskyed pa gcig gis kyang sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa la 'jug go// sems bskyed pa re res kyang yang dag par rdzogs
97a5(phal chen): pa'i sangs rgyas brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa mthong ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rgyun yongs su dag pa la'ang /
97a6(phal chen): rab tu 'jug go// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa yang yongs su ston to// chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ nam mkha'i mthas gtugs par lus byin gyis brlab pa
97a7(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad du khyab pa/ tshad med pa mi gnas pa'ang rab tu shes te/ bdag gi lus de dag la' ba ning thams cad yongs su 'dus par kun tu ston cing / dus gsum gyi sems can

104b4(phal chen): dmigs pa'i tsho gas rab tu spyod pa yin// shin tu yangs pa'i ljags mnga' ba// de dag dbang po rnams dang legs pa'i spyod thos na// su yi sems shig dang mi 'gyur// nam ma
104b5(phal chen): lta bu de dag spyod 'di yin// kun tu mtha' yas shes ldan zhing // chos rnams kun la kun tu mtha' yas mig yod pa// ye shes mtha' yas tshul ldan pa// mtha' yas
104b6(phal chen): shes can de dag spyod 'di yin// zad mi nus pa zang byed cing // bsod nams 'byam klas yod pas bsod nams mi zad pa// 'gro ba dag pa'i mthar phyen rnams// 'dra med de dag
104b7(phal chen): spyong pa 'di yin no// tshogs dang ldan ning 'jig rten dang // de dag chos kyi lam la rab tu 'jug byas kyang // de dag sems can 'du shes med// sems can bye ba khrag khrig rab tu
105a1(phal chen): 'grel// nyon mongs med pa rtogs shes shing // spyod pa mngon par shes pa thams cad mthong ba'i rnams// bde ba'i lam rnams ston byed pa// mig
105a2(phal chen): can de dag tshul ni 'di yin no// sangs rgyas ye shes spyod pa dang // tshad med yon tan dam pa thob par gyur pa'i rnams// mi 'jigs pa ni rnyed gyur pa// shes can de dag tshul
105a3(phal chen): ni 'di yin no// 'jug pa kun la rab zhugs shing // zhing la 'jug dang chos kyi dbang la zhugs gyur pa// sems can nugs la gnas byas nas// sems can dam pa sems can
105a4(phal chen): 'grol bar byed// phyogs rnams kun tu chos kyi rnga// brdungs shing 'jig rten 'di dag ston byed pa'i// chos rab sbyin pa'i bdag po rnams// nyams med rtogs byed de dag spyod
105a5(phal chen): 'di yin// skyil mo krung 'dug gcig gis kyang // zhing yangs brjod du med pa kun tu rgyas byed kyang // su yi lus la gnod byed pa// chos sku ldan pa de dag spyod 'di yin// don dang /
105a6(phal chen): yi ge gcig la yang // shin tu bstan pa bye ba khrag khrig rjes su 'brang // de dag mtha' ni rnyed mi nus// mnyam med shes ldan de dag spyod 'dri yin// bsgribs pa med pa'i tshul
105a7(phal chen): shes pa// sangs rgyas rnam thar tshul la shin tu bslabs pa'i rnams// 'jigs pa med par gyur pa dag/ tshad med de dag tshul ni 'di yin no// de dag phyogs rnams rgya mtsho dang /
105b1(phal chen): zhing rnams rgya mtsho mtha' ma dag dang dbus med pas// shes pa rgya mtsho ldan pa yi// chos rnams rgya mtshos 'jig rten tshim par byed// gang rnams gshegs shing skyer 'gyur dang /
105b2(phal chen): byang chub rnam par 'tshang rgya 'gro ba kun dag tu// su zhig mngon par snang gyur pa// mtha' dbus med pa 'di dag spyod 'di yin// mya ngan 'dra' ba du ma yang // zhing rnams bye ba khrag/
105b3(phal chen): khrig dag ni mngon par snang // 'on kyang smra ba'i seng ge rnams// mya ngan mi 'da' smon lam phyir mi ldog/ chos rnams lhun ni gcig gyur cing // sems can kun dang lus kyang
105b4(phal chen): gcig tu gyur pa'i rnams// rgyal ba dag la rtogs med pas// lus gcig gyur pa spyod 'di yin// tshig dang don rnams tha dad pas// 'jig rten khams rnams mtha' dang
105b5(phal chen): dbus yod ma yin par// rang bzhin gcig la mos pa dag/ dus gsum shes pa dri dag spyod 'di yin// sems can dag dang rgyal ba dang // chos kyi tshul rnams kun la zad pa med
105b6(phal chen): rnyed pa// sangs rgyas byin la mos pa dag/ rgyal bas byin brlabs de dag spyod 'di yin// chags pa med pa'i sku 'dra zhing // chags pa med pa'i mig gi pha rol phyin pa'i rnams/
105b7(phal chen): chags med rna ba mkhas pa dang // chags med yid can de dag spyod 'di yin// mngon shes thams cad rnyed pa dang // ye shes mngon par shes pa'i rjes su song ba'i rnams//
106a1(phal chen): ye shes kun gyi dpal ldan pa// shes pa bzang can de dag spyod 'di yin// shin tu mnyam gzhag sems ldan zhing // ye shes mtha' yas shes rab shin tu/

106a3(phal chen): yid ni yongs su nyams med pa// rtag tu brtson pa de dag spyod 'di yin// kun mkhyen thams cad gzigs pa dag/ sangs rgyas thams cad dus gsum gshegs pa mgon po yi//
106a4(phal chen): rigs dang brgyud du skyes pa'i rnams// rgyal sras de dag spyod pa 'di yin no// rjes su bstan la brtson byed pa// phas kyi rgol ba'i lam la 'jigs med spyod pa dag/ mtha'

106a6(phal chen): thams cad snang bar byed pa'i rnams// mun pa sel ba'i spyod pa 'di yin no// gang du rgyal bas mdzad 'os pa// der ri sems can khrag khrig shin tu 'dul byed cing //

106b1(phal chen): spyod pa thams cad shin tu ston// 'gro bar spyod pa thams cad mthar thug byed// chos kyi dbyings dang mnyam pa yi// bdag gi lus ni brjod du med par gyur pa yis/
106b2(phal chen): de dag legs par brjod byas kyang // bskal pa khrag khrig dag gis mi zad do// yon tan kun tu mtha' yas shing // yon tan mchog rnams thams cad mtha' yas pa'i/

140b2(phal chen): po ma thams cad kyis mo de'i sprin lding zhing 'phrul ba'i rgyan gyis par snang brgyan pa byas so// sangs rgyas la dge bar 'dun pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi gnas med khang grangs med par
140b3(phal chen): rdzas kyi rol mo brdung ba drang dkrol ba thams cad kyi sgra yid du 'ong ba phyung bas bar snang brgyan pa byas so// sangs rgyas skye ba shin tu dkon par dogs pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi na bza' kha
140b4(phal chen): dog sku tshogs pa'i sprin dang na bza' mtshungs pa med pa'i sprin gyi cher 'bab pa'i rgyan gyis bar snang brgyan pa byas so// sangs rgyas la mos pa mtha' yas pa'i sems kyis cod pan
140b5(phal chen): grangs med pa'i sprin las cod pan gyi char chen po 'khor zhing 'brab pa'i rgyan gyis bar snang brgyan pa byas so// sangs rgyas la yid bde ba skyes pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi rin po che kha
140b6(phal chen): dog sna tshogs grangs med pa'i sprin las 'phreng ba sna tshogs kyi char rgyun mi 'chad par 'bab pa'i rgyan gyis bar snang brgyan pa byas so// lha'i bu bye ba brgya stong grangs med pa yang lha
140b7(phal chen): rdzas kyi me tog kha dog tha dad pa grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ me tog zad mi shes pa'i mdzod rab tu bkye nis/ bcom ldan 'das la mngon par gtor to// mos pa'i spos
141a1(phal chen): dri zhim po rnyed cing sangs rgyas la dad par gnas pas/ lha rdzas kyi spos dang bdug pa kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ bcom ldan 'das la
141a2(phal chen): phul lo// rgyan chen po sprul pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi tsan+da dan gyi phye ma kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ bcom ldan 'das la mngon par gtor to// dga'
141a3(phal chen): ba'i sems kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi nam ring du 'brang zhing rin po che'i gdugs kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ bcom ldan 'das la mngon par 'gebs so//
141a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas mtha' yas pa la mos pa'i sems rnam par 'phel bas gos rin po che kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ bcom ldan 'das gshegs pa'i lam gos
141a5(phal chen): kyis yog par byas so// de bzhin gshegs pa la rim gro bya bar mos pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi rgyal mtshan rin po che sna tshogs kyi kha dog can lag na thogs shing / bcom
141a6(phal chen): ldan 'das kyi zham ring du 'dong ngo // sangs rgyas la dga' ba mtha' yas pa rnam par 'phel ba'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi lhab lhub dang phyang phrul kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa'i
141a7(phal chen): yang grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa la phul lo// dad pa mi 'phrogs pa'i sems kyis lha rdzas kyi 'phreng ba grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ bcom ldan
141b1(phal chen): 'das la mngon par gtor ro// mtshungs pa med pa'i dga' ba rnam par 'phel bas lha rdzas kyi bu dan rin po che kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa'i yung grangs med pa lag na thogs
141b2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das kyi drung nas 'dzin to// lha'i bu bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa yang zhi ba la rab tu gzhol zhing bag yod pa tshad med pa'i sems kyis/ lha rdzas
141b3(phal chen): kyi rol mo brdung ba dang dkrol ba kha dog sna tshogs grangs med pa lag na thogs te/ yid du 'ong ba'i sgra dbyangs phyung nas bcom ldan 'das dgyes par byed do// byang chub sems
141b4(phal chen): dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa dgu' ldan gyi gnas nas 'ongs du'i rnams dang / lha rdzas las 'das pa'i mchod pa khams gsum las rnam par 'das pa
141b5(phal chen): dmigs pa'i chos las byung ba/ rjen pa'i dri med pa/ chags pa med pa'i sems tshim par byed pa/ chos kyi tshul zab mos mngon par grub pa/ blo tshad med par yangs pa
141b6(phal chen): las byung ba/ dad pa'i rtsa ba brtun pas rnam par spel ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa las byung ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba dang 'phrul pa grangs med pas mngon par bsgrubs
141b7(phal chen): pa sangs rgyas mchod pa yid kyi rang bzhin las byung ba/ mngon par 'du bya ba med pa'i chos kyi sgo'i rgyas btab pas/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad kun nas yog par byas so//
142a1(phal chen): lha rdzas las 'das pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa las byung ba'i me tog gi bla re sna tshogs kyis chos kyi dbyings kun nas khebs par byas so// lha rdzas las 'das pa
142a2(phal chen): mos pas rnam par dag pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul rgyas par 'gengs pa'i na bza' sna tshogs mngon par dgab pas chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so// chags pa med pa'i
142a3(phal chen): chos kyi rang bzhin rdo rje la yang dag par zhugs pa'i sems kyis/ lha rdzas las 'das pas mi skye ba'i chos las byung ba'i dril bu tshem bur bcad pa'i dra bas chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas
142a4(phal chen): so// chos thams cad sgyu ma lta bur rtogs pa'i sems kyis/ lha rdzas las 'das pa'i spos thams cad kyi mchog gis bdug pa'i rgyan gyis chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so//
142a5(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pas chos kyi dbyings rgyas par bya ba'i sems kyis/ lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che thams cad kyi khri sangs rgyas kyi gdan du bting ba'i rgyan gyis chos kyi dbyings
142a6(phal chen): brgyan pa byas so// sangs rgyas kyi mchod pa rang bzhin 'gag pa med pa'i sems kyis/ lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che sna tshogs kyi rgyal mtshan yang dag par bsgreng ba'i rgyan gyis
142a7(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so// rmi lam lta bu'i chos nyid kyis bsam pa tshim pas/ lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che sna tshogs kyis sangs rgyas kyi pho brang brgyan pas chos
142b1(phal chen): kyi dbyings brgyan pa byas so// mi gnas pa'i dge ba'i rtswa bzang ba med pa las byung bus/ wA DA sA las 'das pa'i rin po che sna tshogs kyi bad+mos kun nas yog pa'i rgyan gyis chos kyi
142b2(phal chen): dbyings brgyan pa byas so// lha rdzas las 'das pa'i spos thams cad kyi mchog gi sprin gyis chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par bya ba dang / me tog kha dog mtha' yas pa sna tshogs
142b3(phal chen): kyi sprin dang na bza' kha dog sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad pa thams cad kyi sprin dang / tsan dan gyi dri zhim po mtha' yas par 'pho ba thams cad kyi sprin dang / lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rin po che
142b4(phal chen): thams cad kyi gdugs rnam pa sna tshogs kyi sprin dang / spos dang bdug pa sna tshogs kyi ngad kun tu ldang ba'i sprin dang / 'phreng ba yid du 'ong ba thams cad kyi sprin dang / lha rdzas las
142b5(phal chen): 'das pa'i lhab lhub rnam par dag pa thams cad kyi sprin dang / byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa rang gi lus gtong ba'i sprin dang / sangs rgyas kyi yon
142b6(phal chen): tan brjod pa las 'das pas bstod cing bsngags pa'i brjod pa zad mi shes pa'i sprin dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i bstod pas brjod pa ji lta ba bzhin du yang dag par bsngags pa'i chos

143a1(phal chen): pas/ chos tshad med pa la gnol ba'i gzungs kyi rgyud thams cad las byung ba'i so so yang dag par rig pa la mkhas pa/ mi zad pa dang mi 'jigs
143a2(phal chen): pas yid dga' bar gyur pa'i rim gro ngoms mi shes pas de bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par bstod pa/ tshig rnam par dbye zhing brjod pas byang chub sems dpa' de dag chos kyi dbyings kyi
143a3(phal chen): lus nam mkha'i khams rgyas par byed pa byin gyis brlabs te/ sangs rgyas 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba thams cad kyis yongs su bzung ba'i yid kyi dbang

169b3(phal chen): ba chos mngon par shes pa/ ye shes rig pa rtsod pa med pa lhur byed pa/ sems can thams cad dge ba'i chos spyod pa la rab tu sbyor ba/ sems can thams cad kyis nyes par sems
169b4(phal chen): bskyed pa la 'khrul pa med pa de yang dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yongs su bsngo ba na/ gnod par byed pa thams cad kyi skyon gyis thogs par mi 'gyur ro// sems can mi bsrun pa'i tshul gyis
169b5(phal chen): ldog par mi 'gyur ro// sems can gyi lta ba'i rnyog pas dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bsngo ba dang 'bral bar mi 'gyur ro// sems can gyi sems 'khrug pas ldog par mi 'gyur ro//
169b6(phal chen): sems can gyi sems kyi rgyud stor bas byang chub sems dpa'i go cha chen po bgros pa las ring bar mi 'gyur ro// 'gro ba thams cad yongs su bskyeb pa'i sngon lam dkrugs ma'i rnyog pa
169b7(phal chen): thams cad kyis bcil bar mi 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i rtsom pa chen po sems can drin du ma gzo ba mthong bas lhod par mi 'gyur ro// byang chub tu dmigs pa'i dge ba'i
170a1(phal chen): rtsa ba sems can mi bsrun pa'i dbang pos zhum par mi 'gyur ro// dge ba'i rtsa ba ji lta ba bzhin las byis pa'i skye bo dang 'grogs pa las 'phang bar mi 'gyur ro//
170a2(phal chen): sems can gzhan gyi skyon gyis skyo bar mi 'gyur ro// / shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo bam po sum cu rtsa gnyis pa// / de ci'i phyir zhe na/
170a3(phal chen): dkyil 'khor 'di ni bsgribs pa med par 'gro ba thams cad rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir 'byung ba ste/ sems can gcig la dmigs shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams bla na med pa
170a4(phal chen): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su bsngo ba ma yin/ 'di lta ste/ zhing rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir zhing gcig la dmigs te/ byang chub sems dpa'
170a5(phal chen): byang chub kyi sems la mngon par spo ba ma yin/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas bsdu ba rnam par dmigs pa'i phyir sangs rgyas gcig la dmigs te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dang
170a6(phal chen): pa skye ba ma yin/ 'di lta ste/ ye shes gcig rjes su rtogs pa'i phyir ye shes gcig la dmigs nas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi smon lam skye ba ma yin gyi/ 'di

184a4(phal chen): ci nas kyang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa chud zos par mi 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang srid pa'i 'du 'jis chud zos par mi 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang sems can gyi khams thams//
184a5(phal chen): cad bsgral ba dang / ci nas kyang skye ba dang 'chi'aphos skyon du mi 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang chags pa med pa'i ye shes kyi sgo stor bar mi 'gyur ba dang ci nas kyang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod/
184a6(phal chen): pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i rgyu zad par mi 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang 'jig rten gyi chos kyis kun tu blangs par mi 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang pha rol tu phyin pa rnams kyis rnam par
184a7(phal chen): dag par 'gyur ba dang / ci nas kyang thams cad mkhyen pa'i stobs phun sum tshogs par 'gyur bar yongs su bsngo ste/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byang chub sems
184b1(phal chen): dpa'i sems bskyed pa mun pa med pa dang ldan pa ni/ chos dkar po snang bar gyur pas nye bar brtan cing yongs su bsngo ba'i mchog skyes bu dam pas spyad pa dang ldan pa dang / yongs su dag
184b2(phal chen): pa'i yid kyis yang dag par rtog pa dang / sems dang 'dra ba'i chos thams cad la zhugs pa dang / sgyu ma dang 'dra ba'i las yongs su shes pa dang / mig yer lta bu'i las kyi rnam par
184b3(phal chen): smin pa la mos pa dang / sprul pa lta bu'i mngon par 'du byed pa la gnas pa dang / sgra brnyan lta bu'i las rten pa dang / grib ma lta bu'i byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i rjes su song ba dang
184b4(phal chen): chags pa med pa'i chos kyi mig rab tu skyes pa dang / bya ba med par 'byam klas pa'i rjes su song ba dang / zhi ba'i rigs rab tu thob pa dang / gnyis su med pa dang ldan pa'i 'dus
184b5(phal chen): byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi chos thams cad la rab tu zhugs pa dang / chos ma nor bu'i mtshan ma thob par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyi rjes su song ba dang
184b6(phal chen): mtshan ma thams cad la zhen pa med pa dang / thun mongs gi las la mkhas pa'i rjes su song ba dang / chos dkar po thams cad rgyun ma chad pa dang / chags pa thams cad kyis
184b7(phal chen): mngon par ma zhen pa dang / chags pa med par 'gro ba la rten pa dang ldan pa yin te/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shin tu bsams pa'i blo dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i

185a3(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ yongs su bsngo ba'i ye shes chen po mngon par shes pa las shin tu rig pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dang ldan pa/ mngon par 'du bya ba med par spyod pa'i sems dge ba dang ldan pa de/ dge

185a5(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du mos shing rjes su song ba'i sems dang ldan par 'gyur bar yongs su bsngo'o// bsngo ba de yang tshad med pa'i ye shes khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir yang dag par mthong //

186b1(phal chen): bskyes bu 'dul ba mchod byas pas// nam yang ngoms par tshor bar mi 'gyur ro// de dag rgyal ba kun la mos byed cing // phyogs rnams kun gyi 'jig rten smon ma'i rnams// mi yi

191a3(phal chen): bas shes rab che ba/ bung ba bzhin du dge ba'i rtsa ba'i tshogs chen po sogs pa/ 'gro ba thams cad las rgyud shin tu 'phags pa/ 'du byed la mngon par zhen pa med pa de bzhin
191a4(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi gdams ngag 'thun par 'dzin pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du ma bsngos pa gang yang med de/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po khyim na gnas
191a5(phal chen): pa'i tshe/ dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag yang dag par sdud cing sgrub bo// yongs su bsngo ste/ de ltar de chung ngu na khyi'i lam gyi rgyud du gtogs pa dang / de ma yin pa'i byol song gi ris su
191a6(phal chen): gtogs pa la zas spu 'ga' 'am/ kham 'ga' yongs su gtong ba byed kyang de thams cad de dag nyid la phan pa dang / de dag nyid la bde ba dang / byol song gi skye gnas de dag
191a7(phal chen): sdug bsngal gyi rgya mche de dag dang / sdug bsngal gyi rgyu de dag dang / sdug bsngal gyi phung po de dag dang / sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba de dag dang / sdug bsngal bsags pa de dag dang /

191b2(phal chen): yongs su sgrol zhing rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o// de la dmigs pas sems can thams cad mngon du byed do// dmigs par byed do// yid la byed do// dge ba'i

212a1(phal chen): pa med do// nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad la'ang rab tu gnas te/ de yang shin tu shes so// bsod nams kyi stobs tshad me pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i skus
212a2(phal chen): chos thams cad gang bar shin tu shes so// sems can thams cad tshim par bya ba'i phyir/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad du 'gro ba la yang dag par spyod do// de'i sems bskyed pa re re zhing yang sems
212a3(phal chen): can brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa stobs bcu'i sar yang dag par 'grub bo// des sems can bsod nams thams cad kyis yongs su gzung zhing thob par bya ba'i phyir/ dge ba'i rtsa ba
212a4(phal chen): rnam par dag pa bsod nams thams cad kyi 'byung gnas dang ldan pa thams cad rab tu sgrub bo// de yo byad ci 'dod pa phun sum tshogs pas bsod nams kyi mdzod yid bzhin gyi nor bu lta bu dang ldan pa
212a5(phal chen): yin no// de gang dang gang du 'gro ba de dang de dag tu zhing thams cad rnam par sbyor zhing 'gro'o// de gang dang gang du spyod pa de dang de dag tu sems can brjod du med pa'i lung brjod du med pa rnam par dag
212a6(phal chen): par bya ba'i phyir/ bsod nams kyi stobs kyis yongs su gzung ba la rab tu gnog cing yang dag par spyod do// de ltar yongs su bsngo ba de la rnam pa de lta bu de'i rgyu mthun pas byang chub sems
212a7(phal chen): dpa'i spyad nga spyod pa na gzugs med pa yin/ 'jig rten thams cad kyis zil gyis mi non pa'i bsod nams can yin// bdu thams cad kyis gzi brjid mi zang po yin phyir rgol pa rnams
212b1(phal chen): cad kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba mi 'phrogs pa yin/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i yid yang dag par rtog pa dang ldan pas smon lam shin tu che ba dang sems rab tu yangs pa yin/ sems bskyed pa gcigs
212b2(phal chen): gis sangs rgyas kyi zhing tshad med par 'gro ba yin/ ye shes kyi stobs mtha' yas pas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul yongs su shes pa yin/ sangs rgyas thams cad la shin tu dad pa yin
212b3(phal chen): ye shes mtha' yas par shin tu 'jug pa la rab tu gnas pa yin/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyis klas pa'i byang chub kyi sems mngon par bsgrubs pa'i mthus nam mkha'i dbyings kyis klas
212b4(phal chen): par chos kyi dbyings shin tu yangs pa yin no// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi yongs su bsngo ba lnga pa bsod nams mi zad pa'i mdzod
212b5(phal chen): ces bya ba ste/ de la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni mi zad pa'i mdzod bcu rab tu 'thob bo// bcu gang zhe na/ skra'i sbubs gcig tu sangs rgyas grangs med pa 'byung ba la 'jug
212b6(phal chen): pa'i phyir sangs rgyas blta ba'i gter mi zad pa'i mdzod rab tu 'thob bo// chos thams cad gcig tu rab tu gzhol ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs dang ye shes kyi phyirachos
212b7(phal chen): la 'jug pa'i gter mi meng pa'i mdzod rab tu 'thob bo// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis chos pastan pa yongs su bcu shing chud mi zos par bya ba'i phyir rnam pas gzung ba'i gtor
213a1(phal chen): mi zad pa'i mdzod rab tu 'thob bo// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi tshul dang dgongs pa shin tu bstan pa la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir/ blo gros rnam par nges
213a2(phal chen): pa'i gter mi zad pa'i mdzod rab tu 'thob bo// chos kyi tshul rnam par dbye ba la mkhas par bya ba'i phyir/ rig pas 'dzin pa'i gter mi zad pa'i mdzod rab tu 'thob bo// nam mkha'i dpying
213a3(phal chen): dang mnyam pa'i blos dus gsum thams cad khyab par bya ba'i phyir/ blo tshad med pa'i gter mi zad pa'i mdzod rab tu 'thob bo// sems can thams cad tshim par bya bas mi zad par bya ba'i phyir/
213a4(phal chen): bsod nams kyi gter mi zad pa'i mdzod rab tu 'thob bo// sems can thams cad kyi mun pa dang / rab ri ba dang / ling tog dang / gti mug dang / ma rig pa'i mun pa rnam par bsal

213a7(phal chen): bskur ba'i phyir/ stobs bcu dang mi 'jigs pa'i gter mi zad pa rab tu 'thob ste/ gter mi zad pa'i mdzod bcu po 'di dag rab tu 'thob bo// de nas byang chub sems dpa'
213b1(phal chen): rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcur rnam par bltas te/ de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// bsam pas mthu stobs rnyed pa de ga ni/
213b2(phal chen): mtha' yas chos la kun tu dbang sgyur zhing // bsod nams gter la rjes su yi rang ba// de dag chags meng tshul gyis yongs su bsngo// dus gsum rgyal ba su dag ji snyed pas// rnam
213b3(phal chen): dag zhing rnams 'jig rten rnam stu sri pa// yon tan kun dang ldan zhing 'phags pa'i rnams// de 'dra'i rnam dag zhing du yongs su bsngo/ gdus gsum rgyal ba ji skad bzhugs pa yi// tshul
213b4(phal chen): rnams kun la rjes su sems byed cing // thams cad lus pa med par des bzung ste// de 'dra'i zhing ni brtan pa rnams kyis brgya nA// dus gsum bskal pa ji snyed yod pa yi// zhing gcig
213b5(phal chen): yon tan de dag blang byas kyang // bskal pa ji snyed de dag zad 'gyur gyi// zhing gi yon tan bsngags pa zad mi 'gyur// 'di 'dra'i zhing rnams thams cad ma lus par// mi yi mchog gis
213b6(phal chen): ji snyed mthong gyur pa// tham sa cad ma lus zhing gi yon tan gyis// ji snyed 'jig rten de dag brgyan par snang // de dag kun kyang rnam dag yid dang ldan// de dag rgyal ba'i gsung skyes

214a2(phal chen): thob/ mtshungs med shin tu rnam par dag pa'i yid// thams cad phyogs rnams su ni 'od kyang 'gyed// 'di 'dra'i zhing rnams ma lus gzung byas te/ nyan thos spyod yul dag la dad med pa//

214b1(phal chen): rlung / yod pa'ang ma yin med pa'ang ma yin te// rgyu yi rgyud la mngon par chags mi byed// rkyen la'ang 'jug par de dag mi byed de// nam yang de dag chags par mi byed do// 'gro ba 'di na snga

260b4(phal chen): leg gi sbyin pa byed cing yongs su gtong ba'i tshe/ dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag sems can thams cad la 'di ltar yongs su bsngo ste thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du dmigs te/ rkang lag yongs
